Less than five minutes into the battle, Fudan's Wang Shusen accidentally headed the ball into his own goal while trying to save it. Jinan was overjoyed, while Fudan was frustrated. After Jinan scored this goal, their spirit was even more invigorated. About five minutes later, Fudan was penalized with a penalty kick. Chen Zhenhe kicked the ball, and within ten minutes, Jinan scored two goals in a row. Fudan only had themselves to blame.

Jinan's Goal Was Breached

Fudan was very unfortunate to lose these two goals, and they rallied their spirits, aiming to expand their grand plan. Jinan's Qiu Dongyan intended to save the ball, but it hit Feng Han You's back. Goalkeeper Jiang Zongjin tried to save it but was unable to. Fudan's Gong Yixun saw the opportunity and rushed up to shoot the ball into the goal. Fudan scored a goal in return, and the morale was boosted. They fought again, but Jinan was unwilling to show weakness and resisted. Fudan ultimately could do nothing. Chen Baomiao once advanced but returned without success. Yun Shijian Mei Hongbao dribbled the ball and passed it to the center. Chen Zhenxiang intercepted it and, in the midst of the melee, Chen attacked and scored into the Fudan goal. The first half ended with a score of three to one, with Jinan taking the lead.

Little Mei Played Well

The sound of the restart was heard, and Jinan's soldiers invaded the enemy camp. Mei Hongbao changed his feet nimbly and made a great contribution. The ball hit the crossbar and bounced into the net, impossible to save. It was only three minutes after the start of the second half. At this time, Fudan's goalkeeper, Qu Hongde, arrived late and immediately entered the arena in uniform to guard the goal. Fudan's courage was greatly boosted, and the forwards pressed Jinan. Sun Huipei had a chance, but unfortunately, he was too hasty and went out of bounds, which was a pity. Jinan's army once again surrounded Fudan, and Qu Hongde became the target of everyone and was exhausted from dealing with it. Fortunately, Guan Xun An guarded the line well, and there was no loss.

The Result Was Five to One

In the midst of the melee, Chen Zhenhe and Li Lin had a small conflict, but they did not resort to violence. The referee and players from both sides mediated to stop it. Fudan counterattacked again but made no achievements. Instead, Jinan's Chen Zhenhe dribbled the ball deep into Fudan's goal, about a dozen yards from the goal, and shot from a distance. The ball rolled towards the goal, very fast. Fudan's goalkeeper Qu used his feet instead of his hands, and the ball rolled into the net under his legs. Qu made a big mistake, leading to a major mistake. As a result, Jinan won with a score of five to one.

Again in the Final Against Jiaotong University

Jinan won easily yesterday, controlling the whole game. Fudan's talents were average, but because they had to go to Beijing to petition today, they were too hasty in the battle and very timid. Their experience was also relatively poor and not as bold as Jinan's. The wings were very weak, and the three center forwards were very good. Li Lin had a special performance. Jinan has faced Jiaotong University in the final for many years, and today is the same. It's a real feud.

Free Talk

The Voice of Resistance Against Japan

— Liang

Cheng De Gao, father of Cheng Feng Shan, a correspondent dispatched by this newspaper from Changhuaiwei, Bengbu, whose courtesy name is Yangzhi, is sixty-six years old this year, and has always enjoyed books and history. Because he read in the Shen Bao about Chairman Ma's heroic resistance against Japan in Heihe, he lectured the people daily, often weeping bitterly. Later, upon hearing that Ma's army had retreated to Keshan, he slammed the table and shouted loudly, his face suddenly turning pale. He then recited a poem of farewell: "Who will support the collapsing mansion? The vast land of China is like a sleeping lion. Tell my children to listen to my last words: remove the strong and repay your old father." After reciting, he sighed deeply, and his breath ceased. This old man's love for his country and his martyrdom must be recorded.

Bu Ting Qi Talks About Removing Weeds

The Children's Chicken (Part Two)

A Letter to Xu Jun Qizhou

I suspect you may have already thought about the later stages of development, but perhaps due to environmental obstacles, you have been forced to stop at the second stage. For this, we of course have considerable understanding. Mr. Fan Jingsheng once told me that in the past, at the Capital University, because a Japanese instructor dissected a sheep in the classroom for the students, it aroused the Empress Dowager's great anger, and the Minister of Education Zhang Baixi was so anxious that he entered the court to kowtow and request punishment. This is similar to your chicken hatching. However, in civilized Shanghai, something like "School is an important place, chickens are not allowed" will probably not happen, right? Therefore, I urge you to muster your courage and do it.

The first stage of education will not even bloom a flower, let alone bear fruit! The second stage of education will only bloom flowers, but not bear fruit. It is not until the third stage that it will bear fruit, but the fruit may not be delicious and large. To have delicious and large fruit, one must jump to the fourth stage. The fourth stage is the ultimate in the integration of teaching, learning, and doing: it has already become one with science here.

Let's take the children's chicken as an example. Hatching chickens is an essential activity. If you raise two groups of chickens: one group with a rooster, and one group without a rooster, and mark the eggs laid by the two groups of chickens, hatch them, and see which group's eggs hatch into chicks, that would be even better. Furthermore, dissect the eggs that have been incubated for three days, five days, seven days, nine days..., to see what changes have taken place in each egg, and create a set of specimens from the development of the egg to the chick, wouldn't that be even more interesting? Furthermore, comparing the egg-laying ability and inheritance of various chickens can gradually be promoted in elementary schools. Of course, elementary schools have other subjects, not chicken hatching research institutes, so how much can you do? But hatching a few chickens and making a few sets of specimens can't be considered wishful thinking. You are an experienced elementary school teacher, do you think what I have described is correct? I hope you will not hesitate to give me your advice. I wish you success in leading the children to attack nature. ...

The Unknown Hero in the Sino-Japanese War of 1894-1895

— Zheng Yimei

In the Sino-Japanese War of 1894-1895, although our country did not win, there were indeed some heroes who loyally gave their lives, enough to glorify the annals of history, such as Deng Shichang and Zuo Baogui. I once heard my friend Mingdao Gu Zi talk about an anecdote of an unknown hero, Zhu Tieqiang (Iron Spear), in that war. My friend is a talented writer, and perhaps he has already recorded it in his books, but I have not had the opportunity to see it. Now, I will describe what I have heard below, as a model for comrades resisting Japan. Zhu Tieqiang lost his name. From childhood, he was extremely brave and unparalleled, good at using a spear. When he danced, he moved up, down, left, and right, spinning like flying. The faster he danced, the faster it became, only seeing a ball of white light, not seeing the person. If a giant urn of water was poured on him, there would be no drop on his collar, because the light and air tightly surrounded him, with no gaps to enter. Therefore, he had the nickname Zhu Tieqiang. When the Sino-Japanese War started, Tieqiang rose up and joined the command of Zuo Baogui, winning many victories. Baogui quickly rewarded his strength and promoted him. In the Battle of Pyongyang, Tieqiang and Zuo each led an army to fight the Japanese pirates. The Japanese had long heard of Zhu's courage and were angry at the number of people he had killed, so they launched a large-scale attack to take revenge. Tieqiang rode his horse and galloped, killing hundreds and thousands of Japanese again. But the enemy was numerous and he was outnumbered. The Japanese soldiers surged like a tide. Zhu's army suffered countless casualties, and the corpses piled up into a Jingguan (mound of corpses). Tieqiang still did not retreat slightly. Some advised him, but Tieqiang's eyes were wide open and his canthus were about to split, and said, "A true man should die in battle, wrapped in horsehide. I have no regrets." Then Tieqiang rushed out of the formation to rescue Zuo who was surrounded. At that time, only three or four hundred cavalry followed Tieqiang. Tieqiang led them to fight one against a hundred, rescuing Zuo from the central army. The Japanese's left and right wings attacked, and giant cannons fired shells, like the rumbling of thunder. The smoke and gunpowder obscured vision. Tieqiang was not afraid at all. After fierce fighting, he was finally killed by the Japanese emperor's third nephew. The Japanese hated Tieqiang even more. The soldiers surrounded him tightly. During the struggle between Tieqiang and Zuo, a merciless bullet hit Tieqiang's elbow, breaking it and causing blood to flow profusely, changing the color of the sandy desert. He and Zuo died together. Even in his dying moments, he shouted loudly to kill the Japanese, not stopping. Those who heard it were moved. The Japanese and our China have a long-standing feud. This time, they have trampled on the Northeast, treating our people like meat on a chopping board. If we do not rise up to resist them, the country will not exist, and where will the people be attached? Zhu Tieqiang, if your soul is conscious, you must be weeping in the nine springs.

A New Invention to Avoid Airplane Deaths Using Wireless Radio

— Huang Yingdai

The airplane, although it is the only important means of transportation in modern times, since its invention, the number of people who have sacrificed their lives due to aviation is countless. Recently, such as the Chinese poet Xu Zhimo, also died in an aviation accident. Therefore, European and Western countries pay close attention to the issue of aircraft accidents, hoping to reduce the danger to the lives of aviators. London is developing a method to reduce aircraft accidents by using wireless radio to transmit messages. After this method is implemented, it can save the lives of many aviators. What is this method? It is to predict drastic weather changes and use wireless radio to transmit messages. Even a thousand miles away, if a hurricane suddenly rises, the weather instrument can detect waves and report the news. The inventor of this method is an Englishman named Wass. This device can be placed in a small house. A thousand miles away, even a small electric light is emitted. This weather instrument can use wireless radio to jump into the darkness and then use eyesight to observe. The discovery of hurricanes in the Atlantic Ocean, Central Asia, and Asia can be seen at a glance. The strength of the wind and the height of the air temperature are all recorded. This device has a special and amazing feature, that is, it can express 3,000 kinds of symbols in one second. Therefore, weather observers can always point out where the storm originates. There are two observatories in northern England and Scotland, which cooperate with each other to make the start and stop and location of gales and rainstorms clearer. Then, the results are reported to the aviators, so that they can prepare early and not collide with the storm, so that the number of accidents can also be reduced.

World News in Brief

Restrictions on British University Students

Students at Oxford University in England are subject to very strict restrictions. Even when renting a car, they are not allowed to exceed one hour each time. If it is necessary to exceed this time, they must obtain the permission of the president.

Child Marriage in New York Child marriage in New York is gradually increasing, shocking the local authorities. According to a survey, there were 552 elementary school students who got married in the past year. Among them, one groom was only fourteen years old, and the bride was only twelve years old.

Glass House in Paris A new building in Paris is based on a steel skeleton. Except for the bathroom, of course, the rest of the rooms are made entirely of glass. The four sides are transparent and do not block the light, which is particularly abundant, like a crystal palace in a myth.

Canaries Enter the United States The city of Norwich in England produces a large number of canaries (in Chinese, they are commonly called hibiscus birds). Every year, as many as 10,000 birds are imported into the United States. Bird lovers must keep one. The singing ones cost up to fifty shillings.

Casual Talks From Di Xiang Zhai

— Gan Dang

Cen Chi (Continued)

Chi respectfully replied, "Your daughter was born in a noble family, while I am a poor scholar. It is not a match." His late uncle said, "A gentleman is steadfast in poverty, a principle you have always adhered to. With such talent and learning, your future fame and position will surpass mine. Why do you use poverty as an excuse?" Sincere words were spoken from the heart. After careful consideration, they finally agreed to the marriage. He was appointed as Second Magistrate by donating grain, and entered the staff of Tao Mo, the Governor-General of Shaanxi and Gansu, and was appointed as the magistrate of Chang'an County through Mo's recommendation. He met Cen Chunxuan, the Provincial Treasurer, through Mo's introduction. Chunxuan's ancestors were originally from Zhejiang. In terms of seniority, he was a cousin. Over time, the two became closer. Chi was honest, upright, and had exceptional insight and judgment. After Chunxuan was promoted to Governor of Shaanxi, Mo planned to retire and return to his hometown, so he welcomed Chi to live in the governor's residence as his teacher, consulting him on everything before acting. From then on, from Jin to Shu to Liang Yue, Chi never left his side. According to the custom, at the end of the year, the staff of the governor's office could request a formal appointment for their officials, which is called "Ba'an" (recommendation). Chunxuan always placed Chi's name at the beginning of the memorial, but Chi often crossed it out with his pen, displeased, and said, "This is not what I want. It cannot be forced." Chunxuan thought he was being modest and asked him. Chi said, "I look at myself in the mirror and see that wealth and fame are not for me." Chunxuan laughed and said, "You were once a Second Magistrate, weren't you an official?" Chi said, "That is enough." Xuan knew that his will could not be changed and never mentioned it again. Chi supported Xuan's measures that were appropriate and reasonable, and did not hesitate to praise them. Conversely, he would argue face to face without any leniency. Xuan usually did not give in to anyone's words, regardless of whether they were appropriate or not, but he regarded Chi as a good teacher and friend, listening to his words and following his advice. The memorials impeaching Yikuang and others were all written by Chi. When the Xinhai Revolution broke out, Xuan was reappointed as the Governor of Sichuan and telegraphed to summon Chi. Chi did not go. He insisted on requesting it. Then he crossed the ferry to Hanfu and told Xuan, "The world is about to be in great chaos. This is just a slight glimpse of it. You decide for yourself whether to advance, retreat, go out, or stay. I am old and cannot accompany you." Then he returned home. After returning, he disguised himself as a Taoist priest, wandering in the mountains and springs, singing poems for pleasure. One year, he leaned on his cane to climb Mount Tai and visited the sage Confucius in Qufu, sighing and lamenting, "The Great Dao has not been practiced for a long time. The great chaos in the world is not far away. I cannot bear to witness it." He died at the age of seventy-odd. His son, Jiao Lin, was able to inherit his family learning, and was pure and resembled his father. In the late Qing Dynasty, he knew Anwei Wuwei Prefecture. In the Republic of China, he served as a tax official and magistrate of Wujin, taking not a single hair's breadth dishonestly. After a man of virtue, there must be talented people. I am even more convinced of this.

A Spirited Anti-Japanese Banquet

— Yanzi

Since the brutal Japanese invasion and occupation of Liaoning and Jilin, patriotic people in our country have been running around, calling for unity against Japan. Mr. Sun Xueni, the owner of Sheng Sheng Fine Arts Company, has always been enthusiastic about saving the country, fearing that foreigners will accuse him of having a five-minute fever. He specially produced a set of five-color anti-Japanese calendars, painted by his talented student Tian Qingquan and inscribed by his friends He Tianjian, Yu Yifen, and others. They are shocking and can serve as a wake-up call for the people of our country, hoping that every household will have one and keep it in mind forever. The intention is good and appreciated by all. Yesterday was the date of the company's banquet for guests, and I was also among those invited. The banquet was held at Liuheju on Guangxi Road. On the windows facing the road, the words "Sheng Sheng Company Anti-Japanese Banquet on the Second Floor" were written in large red paint. Inside the building, the walls were covered with more than ninety kinds of various five-color embossed calendar baseboards produced by the company, and thirty-one anti-Japanese calendars. Before long, well-known figures from the political, business, and academic circles in Shanghai gathered one after another. Xueni and his younger brother Guangdi greeted them and showed them to their seats, distributing anti-Japanese calendars and a set of embossed calendars and anti-Japanese postcards produced by the company. First, Mr. Sun reported the purpose of printing this anti-Japanese calendar for anti-Japanese propaganda, and advertisements welcoming domestic goods were not charged. Thousands of words were eloquent and appropriate. His painstaking efforts moved those who heard it. Then, guests Chen Xuyuan, Lu Fengzhu, Qian Shoutie, Wu Zihao, Zhang Zilian, He Tianjian, and others stood up and gave speeches. They were passionate and aroused listeners. Mr. Qian shouted loudly, speaking from the bottom of his heart, extremely painful. Xuyuan's speech was subtle and satirical, using the words "mother-in-law and daughter-in-law" to express the weaknesses of the Chinese people. Only Sheng Sheng Company has the heart of continuous life and death, and fights the enemy. It is truly admirable. If the people of the country could have one set in every home and hang it on the right side of their seats, they could never forget it year after year, day after day, and moment after moment. The attitude was calm during the speech, with the wonder of chatting and joking. The applause from the audience rang out. Commentators said that this old man was romantic and unrestrained, and was indeed extraordinary. He's speech was appropriate in its metaphors, and exposed the worldly customs without leaving anything out, and was better able to awaken the Chinese people's dreams. After the earnest speeches of these famous people, the number of people who placed orders that evening came one after another. It can be seen that the patriotic heart of the people of the country is ten thousand times higher than that of the public officials. By the time the banquet was over, the clock had struck ten.

Rotary Club Novel

Sharing The Enemy (12)

— Gu Mingdao

Chapter 3 Escaping the Tiger's Mouth

When that bullet flew over, fortunately, Hua Naiqiang had quick eyes and immediately squatted down. The bullet swept over his head and missed. Hua Naiqiang took advantage of this opportunity to fire back and knocked the Japanese soldier to the ground. He somersaulted and jumped off the wall. Zhongshu was squatting on the ground. First, she heard the gunshot, then saw Hua Naiqiang jump down, knowing that he had escaped danger. She quickly stood up. Hua Naiqiang said, "That was close. A Japanese soldier chased after me, but fortunately, I killed him. Let's go quickly." So the two fled to a secluded place. At this time, the area was full of Japanese soldiers. The inspection was very strict. The two hid the pistols and Mauser pistols under their clothes to avoid being seen by the thieves and causing obstacles. They thought that they could not go to the city. They should go to T City. But on their way, they had to cross the railway. And that side was stationed by the Japanese army. If they were questioned, it would be difficult to escape. So the two discussed that it was an emergency situation. Fleeing in the daytime was very inconvenient and dangerous. It was better to wait until the evening to leave. For now, they should find a hiding place and avoid it for a while. The two ran a mile or two in the field and saw a low house. An old woman and a seven or eight-year-old boy were looking around in front of the door. The two ran to the front of the house. The old woman first greeted them and asked Hua Naiqiang, "Sir, did you come from the city?" Hua Naiqiang nodded in reply, "Exactly." The old woman said, "The sound of guns and cannons last night almost scared our souls away. This morning, I heard that the Japanese country came to attack our city. We don't know what's going on. My son, Changfu, works as a servant in the city. I don't know how his life is. We are very anxious." Saying this, she pointed to the child with her finger and said, "He is my grandson. He is urging me to take him to see his father." Sir, do you think we have the courage to enter the city?" Hua Naiqiang said, "That's right. Don't go to the city. We also fled from there. The Japanese army is extremely brutal." After Hua Naiqiang finished speaking, the child cried for his father. Zhongshu stepped forward to stop his crying. Hua Naiqiang said to the old woman, "We want to borrow your house to hide for a while. We will flee again at night. Please go in quickly now. Lest they see us and cause trouble." So the old woman led the two inside. The house was very dark and cramped. The two did not care about it and sat down to rest, silently. Although they were not talking at the door, their hearts were full of thoughts and anger, and they were very sad. The old woman brought two cups of tea to respect the guests. Zhongshu said, "Please don't bother. We only need to bother you for two meals. We will thank you heavily when we leave." The old woman said, "Don't rush. Guests, please sit down."

Business News

Financial Gold Standard Declines Weakly

Down Fifteen Taels and a Half

News is Conflicting, Market Extremely Chaotic. Yesterday, the 14th, the gold standard fluctuated dramatically, the decline was quite severe, the market was chaotic, the waves were extremely large, and the momentum was unstoppable. There was a difference of 22 taels throughout the day, and finally, there was a hidden drop of more than fifteen taels. Fellow traders were mentally disturbed and numb, and deposits and withdrawals were very different. The initial opening was a drop, which was really due to the establishment of the new Japanese cabinet, which was about to abandon the gold standard, and the heavy ban on cash exports, as well as the slow payment of war debts, etc., which were enough to affect it. When it broke through 640 taels, then, due to the vigorous purchases by large households from all sides, and it was heard that the League of Nations could resolve the Sino-Japanese issue peacefully, people's hearts turned better, and there was a sudden and rapid increase, which had already broken through the 60 taels mark. However, the trend of foreign exchange was loose and excessive, especially because large households turned around and sold again, so the price could not be sustained, and it was less than 10 taels again. The after-market slightly hovered, but the swap was imminent, and the multilateral intended to knock on a large discount to hold it up. Finally, it was outside of 50 taels, but at this time, the situation was precarious and unstable, so the rise and fall situation was particularly difficult to predict.

Opening Plummets Twenty-Seven and a Half Taels. Since the early opening, there has been a sharp drop of 27 taels and 5 mace, to 642 taels (before the market opened, it was around 40 taels). Both the large bars and the silver price fell by three-eighths from the day before yesterday, but Japan's ban on gold is about to be implemented, so the opening was low. The Dalian gang and others sold a lot, and it continued to drop to 39 and a half taels. Suddenly, it stepped into the clouds, and the numbers moved forward together, such as Taichang Zhifeng Yongcheng Fengyong Yifeng Yongqian Changxiang Yongfeng, etc. all purchased. Especially because the US dollar decreased from 34.0625 yuan to 33.625 yuan, the bank's appetite was still good, and it had already risen sharply by 22 taels, reaching 61 and a half taels. However, there were two or three taels of ups and downs in half an hour. When British gold opened at 25 large, and the US dollar was long at 875, the exchange rate increased greatly, and it had already dropped to 54 taels and 5 mace. Afterwards, it turned around and increased again, and the hedgers came in to calculate 8 and a half taels, but the Dalian gang actually came out, retreating to 2 and a half taels, and the US dollar was still firm. The bank traded 33.5625 yuan, and absorbed 625 again. Also, British gold was 11 pence 6875. Banks had mutual transactions, so it was 59 and a half taels at 10:20. In a moment, Qian Changxiang Zhifeng Yongliang and others sold out, and Mitsui and others bought 8125 for British gold, and in just over ten minutes, it retreated to 53 taels. Unprocessed Tung Oil Market

Since the arrival of new tung oil, prices in various production areas have gradually risen. However, the oil arriving in Hankou is still mostly old oil. This is due to the shallow water levels in the upper reaches of the Yangtze River during the winter, which inevitably causes transportation delays, preventing the new oil from arriving in abundance. The number of foreign firms operating in Hankou remains small. Prices reached 23 taels and 23 mace per foreign standard the previous week but eased slightly to 23 taels to 22 taels and 78 mace per foreign standard last week. Domestic sales by old established oil merchants are priced at 18 taels per foreign standard. Local oil and hemp businesses mainly sell Zhejiang tung oil, so they do not pay much attention to the ups and downs of the Hankou market. When new Zhejiang tung oil first appeared, it was priced at 31 yuan sent to Shanghai per tan, then dropped to 30 yuan. Recently, it has been worth about 29 yuan. It is said that oil mills in the Jin, Qu, Lan, and Yong areas must first press cypress oil, and only after the cypress carriage rush has passed can they start pressing tung oil. Therefore, only a small amount of new oil appears at first, and after the winter solstice, they can all switch to pressing tung oil. According to recent detailed letters from Jin, Lan, and other places, shipments have gradually increased, but the price is still about 28 yuan and several jiao per Lan exchange. If it arrives in Shanghai, it is still around 30 yuan. Therefore, few local businesses are willing to buy, and most are waiting for the price to drop slightly below 29 yuan before entering the market. Since the price has reached this point, there is no need to worry about further declines. However, without large-scale outlets for foreign firms, it is difficult to expect significant improvements. During the arrival of new oil, the market seems to be characterized by prolonged weakness and short-term rallies. Even if there are fluctuations, they will only be within a range of one or two yuan. Local inventories are not abundant, and sales are sluggish due to the winter season. However, preparations for the New Year goods have not yet been made, so a batch of purchases must be made within the lunar year to supply the brisk sales during the New Year season.

Local News

Important Meeting of Beijing-Guangdong Representatives Yesterday

Chen Mingshu Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday Morning and Returned to Beijing Last Night

Sun Ke Discusses the Issue of Contacting Jiang's Resignation

Telegrams to Hu Hanmin and the Guangdong Committee Urge Them to Come to Shanghai Quickly

After Chen Mingshu arrived in Shanghai from Beijing yesterday morning, he visited Sun Ke at Morrie Road at 9:00 AM yesterday to discuss Jiang's resignation and the Guangdong Committee's trip to Beijing. Chen left at 11:30 AM. He originally planned to take a plane back to Beijing at 12:30 PM yesterday to report back, but the plane's parts were damaged, so he changed to a special train at 10:33 PM last night to return to Beijing.

Resignation Telegram According to sources in Guangdong, Chen Youren was also present during the meeting between Chen and Sun. Chen stated that Chairman Jiang had decided to resign and would formally issue a telegram of resignation on the 15th. At the same time, he would submit his resignation to the Central Standing Committee and request that the Guangdong Committee be telegraphed to come to Beijing quickly so that the Fourth National Congress could be convened as soon as possible to produce a unified government. After Chen left, Sun immediately contacted Wu Chaoshu, Li Wenfan, Zou Lu, and others by telephone to discuss and decided to telegraph Hu Hanmin and the Guangdong Committee to come to Shanghai. They dispersed at 1:00 PM.

Transitional Measures As for the transitional measures after Jiang's resignation, the Central Committee Standing Committee will appoint Lin Sen and Chen Mingshu to temporarily act as Chairman of the National Government and President of the Executive Yuan, respectively. The six representatives staying in Shanghai decided to travel to Beijing together two days after Jiang's telegram is issued to prepare for the Fourth National Congress to be held in Nanjing on the 21st of this month.

He Wu Visits Sun He Yingqin and Wu Tiecheng arrived in Shanghai yesterday morning on the same train as Chen Mingshu and others. In addition to visiting Li Wenfan at 2:30 PM to invite the Guangdong representatives to Beijing, He and Wu also visited Sun Zhesheng in the afternoon to talk and invited Sun to invite the six representatives, Wang, Wu, Chen, Zou, and Li, to go to Beijing together to quickly prepare for the first meeting of the Fourth Plenary Session of the Central Committee to be held on the 21st of this month. Wu and He left at 5:30 PM. Sun, Li, Wu, Zou, Chen, and others then drafted a declaration on the current situation and sought Wang's consent. Zou, Wu, and others dispersed at around 6:00 PM.

Sun Ke's Talk After the representatives dispersed, reporters visited Sun Zhesheng. According to him, Chen Zhenru came to Shanghai to report that Jiang had approved the formal telegram of resignation tomorrow (i.e., today) and requested that they go to Beijing. They agreed to go to Nanjing the day after Jiang's resignation (i.e., tomorrow) to prepare for the convening of the first plenary session of the Fourth Central Committee. The meeting has been approved to be held in Nanjing on the 21st of this month. They have telegraphed Guangzhou to ask the committee members to come to Shanghai quickly. He believes that the committee members will rush to leave after receiving the telegram. If the committee members do not arrive in Beijing before the 21st, the opening ceremony will be held first, and they will hold a preparatory meeting to sort out proposals from various parties. As for Jiang's resignation procedures and transitional measures, Jiang will submit his resignation to the Central Standing Committee, and the Central Standing Committee will appoint Lin Sen to act as chairman and Chen Mingshu to temporarily act as president of the Executive Yuan. Military power will likely be taken over by the Ministry of Military Affairs. The remaining items will be announced tomorrow (i.e., today). As for whether Jiang will go to Peiping after his resignation or go elsewhere, it is not yet known. However, it is known that Jiang will attend the Fourth Plenary Session as a member of the Central Committee. Regarding Zhan Tang's arrival in Shanghai, they received a telegram from Hu from Hong Kong the day before yesterday, stating that his blood pressure had increased to 178 degrees, and the doctor instructed him to rest, so he may not be able to come to Shanghai soon. Regarding the incident of French troops causing disturbances on the Yunnan border, when they were in Guangdong, they had received a report stating that French troops and Annamite troops had frequently appeared on the Yunnan and Guangxi borders, and were repairing roads and deploying airfields. The Guangdong side has ordered strict border defense. Zhang Fakui and others can still set off to aid Heilongjiang. This matter was known when he was in Guangdong and will likely be handled by the Fourth Army Group.

Chen Mingshu's Talk Chen Mingshu took a special train back to Beijing at 10:33 last night to report back. This newspaper's reporter interviewed him on the train. According to Chen, the incident of Chairman Jiang's resignation telegram will be discussed and decided after he arrives in Beijing. When asked about the news released by the Guangdong side, Chen's response was extremely vague, saying only, "Wait and see the facts before discussing, there is no need to rush."

Declaration Postponed Yesterday afternoon, the Guangdong representatives decided to jointly publish a statement on the political views after national unification, signed by 31 committee members, including Wang Jingwei, Sun Ke, Wu Chaoshu, Li Wenfan, Zou Lu, Chen Youren, Ju Zheng, Qin Zhen, Xie Chi, Li Liejun, Cheng Qian, Xiong Kewu, Chen Gongbo, Gu Mengyu, Jing Hengyi, Chen Jiayou, Chen Bijun, Liu Luyin, Fang Zhenwu, Gan Naikang, Zhang Zhiben, Fu Rulin, Mao Zuquan, Wang Faqin, Bai Yunti, Pan Yunchao, Zhu Jiqing, Guo Chuntao, Zhao Pilian, Liang Hancao, and Zeng Zhongming. However, because Wang Jingwei did not attend, the original draft was sent to Wang for review. However, after 10:00 PM, Zeng Zhongming and Liu Luyin went back and forth between Wang and Sun to discuss it many times, and it still needed to be revised, so a decision could not be made. Therefore, the declaration was suspended from publication. However, according to Liu Luyin, it may still be published tomorrow.

The First Batch of Demonstrating Groups from Various Universities Went to Beijing Yesterday

More Than 500 People Departed First

Taking Ordinary Passenger Trains to Beijing

Order and Spirit Were Neat

Representatives of the demonstrating groups from various universities in the city gathered at the North Station at 10:00 AM yesterday. By 2:00 PM, the demonstrating groups from various schools had arrived one after another, totaling more than 500 people. An emergency meeting of representatives was convened at the temporary office of the group at the North Station to discuss everything and contact the transportation matters. Representatives from the Telecommunications School and four other schools were appointed to negotiate with Guo Chengen, Director of the Railway Bureau. As a result of the discussion, they were allowed to go to Beijing on passenger trains as a sign of accommodation. The departure was allowed at 4:30 PM. Fifty members of the Fudan University Military Police maintained order in the station. The group members all wore uniforms, and the commanders of each school wore white armbands. The General Affairs Office prepared a general flag with the words "Shanghai University Student Demonstration Group," which was very eye-catching. About thousands of people from all walks of life came to watch and send them off, and the order was well-maintained. At about 5:00 PM, the representatives of each school and the Fudan Military Police returned to their respective schools, and their spirits were quite radiant and solemn. The details of their departure are recorded below:

Persuasion Ineffective Cai Yuanpei telegraphed Wang Boqun and others from Beijing the day before yesterday, asking them to relay to the presidents of various universities to dissuade the students from going to Beijing. The original telegram read: Rong, Director of the Telegraph Bureau, please immediately forward to Wang Boqun, Zhang Yongni, Li Denghui, Deng Hongnian, Wang Jingqi, Li Zhaohuan, Hu Shuhua, He Shizhen, Zheng Yuxiu, Chu Fucheng, Liu Zhanen, Cao Liangxia, Liu Haisu, Pan Gongzhan, and other gentlemen. According to reports, one-third of the students in Shanghai are scheduled to enter Beijing in the cold weather. Now that the diplomacy has temporarily come to an end after accepting the resolution of the League of Nations, the content and the government's difficulties have been announced. As for domestic affairs, the Fourth Central Committee will soon gather in Beijing to produce a unified government. Coming to Beijing at this time will inevitably have no results. The weather in Beijing has suddenly turned cold, below freezing, and living is difficult. Please invite the presidents and professors of various schools to find ways to dissuade the students from coming to Beijing, and report the progress of the negotiations by telegram. Cai Yuanpei, brother. After receiving this telegram, the presidents of various schools tried to dissuade the students the night before last and yesterday morning, but the students' determination to go was firm, and there was no effect. They resolutely went to Beijing.

Contacting Vehicles At 12:00 AM, representatives from Guanghua contacted Guo Chengen, Director of the Two Railway Bureaus, regarding vehicles for the demonstrating group going to Beijing. According to the response, they received an edict from Chairman Jiang last night (i.e., the 13th) stating that all student groups going to Beijing were not allowed to be released, and no one was allowed to ride the train without a ticket. Violators would be dealt with by military law. If the students insisted on taking the train to Beijing today, the vehicles would be destroyed and not allowed to depart. This was to comply with the edict. Since the negotiation for vehicles by the demonstrating group yielded no results, an emergency meeting of representatives was convened. Fudan, Telecommunications, Liangjiang, and Merchant Marine schools were appointed to be responsible for negotiating with the director of the Railway Bureau. Seeing the strong feelings of the crowd, the director felt unable to stop them by force. As a result of the discussion, a compromise was reached. Since the number of people in the group going to Beijing this time was not large, they could ride on passenger trains. However, the group had to acknowledge that they were forcing their way onto the train, and the bureau would not be responsible for any military intervention or other incidents along the way. The railway could only release as many vehicles as possible for those going to Beijing tomorrow, still operating as passenger trains. If special trains were to be opened, it would be difficult to approve. After the negotiations were completed, the demonstrating group going to Beijing drove away on passenger trains at 4:30 PM.

Number of People Going to Beijing Fifty people from the Law School (Fifth Team), Commander Wang Shouchang; forty people from Xinhua Art Academy (Seventh Team), Commander Zhang Ruohan; two hundred and twenty people from Tongji (Ninth Team), Commander Wang Yunpu; one hundred and fifty people from Jiaotong University (Tenth Team), Commander Gong Shaoxiong; sixty-seven people from Telecommunications (Thirteenth Team), Commander Wang Chuan geng; ten people from Sino-French Institute of Technology (Twenty-fourth Team), Commander Chen Guohan; seven people from Vincent School, Commander Li Peiji; and seven people from the Liangjiang Rescue Team, Team Leader Li Chongxian, a total of eight schools with more than 500 people.

List of Representatives Chen Kan, Liu Chuanzhong, and Shen Zurui from the Law School; Pan Chuji and Li Zhang from Fudan; Sheng Yuhua and Yao Wanruo from Liangjiang; Hu Sizhai and Jin Xihan from Culture; Gu Wenkui, Bi Shilin, and Zhang Haoran from Central Business School; Xu Jia and Liu Liangzhan from Jiaotong University; Yao Jinzhu, Yu Naigang, Wang Wenyun, Li Ya, and Shen Zengshun from Telecommunications; Fan Yibang and Lai Yifu from Zhonggong; Gu Mingxue and Wang Xianlun from Art School; Shi Luzong from Chizhi; Xu Zhucen and Zhu Dian from China Medical College; Huang Xi and Song Suichang from Tongji Engineering College; Liu Lianzhong and Chen Mingzhao from Merchant Marine; Gu Pei and Xiao Qianshi from Tongji Medical College; Gu Jiwu and Liu Zhujing from Jiangnan; Chen Yuejiang and Liang Meichu from Sino-French Institute of Technology; Lin Zuyu from Guanghua; Yuan Zhongxing and Wu Zaiguang from Xinhua; and Xie Yanqing from Daxia. List of Staff General Commander Wen Guangyi from Jinan; Deputy Commanders Jin Shijiao from Fudan and Liu Liangzhan from Jiaotong University; Communications Team Leader Gu Licheng from Jiaotong University; Rescue Team Leader Hu Zhiyuan from Tongji; Deputy Team Leaders Zhu Dian from China Physical Education College and Ji Chongxian from Liangjiang; Transportation Office Hu Jinzhu from Telecommunications and Chen Yuejiang from Sino-French; Secretariat Liu Chuanzhong from the Law School; Accounting Office Sun Shian from Culture; and accompanying reporters Guan Zhaowei and Fu Hongxing from Shanghai News Agency.

Meeting of Representatives At 2:00 PM, an emergency meeting of representatives was convened at the temporary office of the demonstrating group of various universities going to Beijing at the North Station. Representatives from 19 schools attended. Tang Gansheng from the Law School presided over the meeting, and Pan Chuji from Fudan recorded the minutes. After the formalities were completed, discussions were held. Matters for discussion and resolution: (1) The Transportation Office, except for Telecommunications, other schools cannot be responsible. How should this be handled? Resolution: Appoint the Law School, Liangjiang, and Fudan to be responsible. (2) Negotiation for vehicles. Resolution: Appoint representatives from Fudan, Telecommunications, Liangjiang, and Merchant Marine to be responsible for negotiating with the Director of the Railway Bureau and the directors of various stations and offices. (3) In addition to Fudan, other schools should be assigned to serve as military police. Resolution: Passed. (4) The meeting of representatives must remain in session until everyone has departed. Resolution: Passed.

Continued Departure The entire demonstrating group will continue to Beijing today, with a total of about 20,000 people. A meeting of representatives will be held at the North Railway Station at 10:00 AM this morning to decide on the policy for going to Beijing. They plan to take the train to Beijing in the afternoon. The joint demonstration of the demonstrating groups in Beijing, Peiping, and Jinan is expected to be realized around the 20th. The group has also decided to organize a rear advisory group after leaving Shanghai to go to Beijing to handle rear affairs.

A Record of the Tragic Destruction of the Dada Company's Dade Steamer

More Than One Hundred People Burned to Death or Drowned

More Than Three Hundred Crew and Passengers Rescued

Second Comprador Burned to Death, Old Engineer Frozen to Death

The Dada Company's Dade steamer, which was traveling from Shanghai to Tongyang, caught fire near Hupu, in a place called Qiwangsha. The entire ship was destroyed. More than one hundred passengers and crew members died after jumping into the river or freezing to death after being rescued. This is the second tragedy for the company after the tragic incident of the Daji. Based on the reporter's investigation, the details are recorded below.

Circumstances of the Fire The Dade steamer's second cabin contained 200 bales of foreign flannel and American cotton, surrounded by more than 400 bags of white sugar. It departed from Shanghai at 1:30 AM on the 13th of this month. It was near Hupu in Changshu, in a place called Qi Huangsha, at 11:40 AM. The crew, sailors, and passengers on the ship were having lunch when smoke suddenly appeared in the cotton cabin. The crew did not know about the fire at first. When it was discovered, black smoke rushed upwards. The sailors immediately reported to the shipowner, Le Changming, who quickly sought to put out the fire. The ship gathered all the crew and sailors, and each took leather belts and firefighting equipment to draw water to spray. By this time, the fire had already broken through the cabin surface and was burning the deck.

Strong Wind and Fierce Fire The two-story deck was made of wooden boards, which ignited immediately. Seeing that the water spraying was ineffective, the shipowner and others took the fire extinguishing chemicals prepared on the ship for emergency use and sprayed them. However, the weather was extremely cold that day, and the wind was particularly strong. After the fire burned the two-story cabin, it spread extremely quickly with the help of the wind. Although there were fire extinguishing chemicals and water from leather belts, they were completely ineffective. After 12:00 PM, the entire two-story cabin was on fire. At this point, the shipowner and others were helpless.

Raising the Flag for Help Shipowner Le Changming frantically pulled the rescue whistle, hoping that passing ships would assist in the rescue, but no one responded. In desperation, they raised the rescue flag again. Meanwhile, crew members risked smoke and fire to reach the upper deck, intending to lower small sampans to rescue the passengers on board. However, before the ropes suspending the sampan could be untied, the fire had already reached the upper deck.

Passengers Jumping into the River According to the company's investigation, the Dade steamer sold tickets for 340 passengers, and about 100 passengers bought tickets after boarding the ship. There were about 120 employees, including crew members and sailors, on the ship, for a total of more than 500 people. After the fire broke out, everyone scrambled in different directions, trying to escape. They rushed to the top of the ship, wanting to release the sampan. However, when the fire reached the upper deck, the passengers, with no way out, jumped into the river, hoping to escape. Many drowned on the spot, and many died from the severe cold.

Driving the Ship Aground Seeing that the entire ship was on fire and beyond repair, the shipowner quickly accelerated and drove the ship into the shallow waters of Qi Huangsha, grounding the ship and then attempting to rescue the passengers. Fortunately, the Taikoo Company's Yichang, Xiangtan, Yihe, and Hehe ships passed by, saw the Dade's rescue flag raised high, and sent sampans into the river to rescue the people who had fallen into the water.

Various Ships Assisting in the Rescue First, two sandboats, seeing the Dade on fire, quickly released four sampans to the Qi Huangsha riverside to salvage the passengers who had fallen into the water. Then, the Yichang, Xiangtan, and Pinghe also released one sampan each, heading to the side of the Dade steamer to rescue the people who had fallen into the water. At 8:00 PM that night, the Shanghai Dada Company received a telegram from Tongzhou, stating that the Yichang and other sampans had rescued more than 100 people, who had landed in Tongzhou. The Xiangtan had also rescued many people, who were to land in Taixing. In Tongzhou, three people had already frozen to death.

Distressed Passengers Arrive in Shanghai According to the company's report, a total of 205 people were rescued by the sandboats. Yesterday morning, the Victoria tugboat, which was sent by Jardine Matheson to the scene of the accident to assist in the rescue on behalf of the customs, brought the sandboat to Shanghai at about 9:00 AM. They all landed in Wusong. Some had already taken the train to Shanghai, and the rest were transported by sandboat. There were also eight bodies, seven men and one woman, which were sent to the Life-Saving Association for burial. At 7:00 PM, another two people who had been rescued on the sandboat outside Wusong were brought by the water patrol team's small steamer and are now being accommodated by the company. Yesterday, the Daqing arrived and also rescued eight people.

Crew Deaths The acting shipowner, Le Changming, and the accountant and five others were rescued by another sandboat to Liuhe and came to Shanghai yesterday to report everything to the company. The comprador, Qi Baorun, had already gone to Yang and did not board the Dade steamer, while the second comprador, Shen Yuncheng, had been burned to death. The old engineer, Xin Lishan, jumped into the river at the time and froze to death after being rescued. Other drivers, sailors, cooks, and tea room staff were either burned to death or drowned. According to people in the company yesterday, the exact number of deaths is unknown, but it is estimated that about 30 people died.

The Ship is Completely Destroyed After the Dade steamer caught fire, the Shanghai company immediately sent the Dayu steamer to assist in the rescue yesterday morning, while Nantong sent the Chuyuan tugboat to assist in everything. Yesterday, the Shanghai Bureau received a follow-up telegram stating that the entire Dade steamer had been burned to a shell. The 200 pieces of American cotton, 400 bags of white sugar, 200 pieces of water tobacco, and other sacks and miscellaneous goods in the cabin were also completely burned. The ship's shell is still stranded in the shallow waters of Qi Huangsha. The Dade steamer has a deadweight of 800 tons and was built in 1891. The loss of the ship and goods is estimated to be between 300,000 and 400,000, and more than 100 passengers and crew members died in the fire.

Company Notice The Dada Company issued a notice to merchants yesterday: "We hereby inform you that our company's Dade steamer, on the schedule of December 12, departed on the evening of 1:30 AM, heading to Tongyang and other places, carrying a total of 1,052 pieces of passenger goods. Unfortunately, at 11:43 AM on the 13th, an accident occurred in Qiwangsha, and all rescue efforts were ineffective. The entire ship was destroyed, leaving only the ship's shell. The Dayu Chuyuan has been sent to the scene of the accident to find ways to tow it back to Shanghai. Please send someone to inspect it. This is a special notice."

Handling of the Aftermath Since receiving the warning telegram the night before last (the 13th), the Nantong branch has been trying to rescue. Shanghai has also sent the Dayu and Chuyuan tugboats, carrying necessary clothing and bedding. It is believed that they have arrived at the scene of the accident. However, in front of the 16th Pier yesterday, the families of the crew members and relatives of the passengers were asking questions, and the crowd was extremely crowded. Some even had confirmed news that their loved ones had already died in the fire or drowned, and they wailed and collapsed on the ground, and the passersby were saddened. The company is carrying the bodies and sending them to the Tongren Fuyuantang for coffin burial. The surviving passengers are being registered by the Jiaotong Chongru Township Association. Because most of them are anxious to go home, the passengers who were rescued and returned to Shanghai and landed in Songjiang did not wait to register and left first. Therefore, it is impossible to confirm who is alive and who is dead. The Daqing, which arrived yesterday, did not rescue any personnel. It is said that there will be accurate information on how many died when the Daiwa arrives in Shanghai today.

Joint Declaration by District Party Headquarters

Denial of the Party Affairs Improvement Committee

The First, Second, Fifth, Sixth, Ninth, and Tenth District Party Headquarters of this city yesterday jointly declared their denial of the so-called Party Affairs Improvement Committee. They stated, "Having seen in the newspapers a news item about an emergency meeting of city-wide party members convened at the College of Law and Politics, we are deeply astonished. Aside from the fact that the meeting was attended by only thirty or forty people, and that many non-party members were mixed in, which disqualifies it as a city-wide party member meeting, according to the procedures, a city-wide party member meeting can only be convened upon the instruction of the Central Executive Committee, or when the Municipal Executive Committee deems it necessary, or when more than half of the District Executive Committees deem it necessary, and is convened by the Municipal Executive Committee as a temporary meeting. According to the general regulations, a meeting is convened annually. Now, the relevant agencies have not heard of any intention to convene the so-called city-wide party member emergency meeting. Therefore, the meeting is fundamentally illegal, and is clearly a reactionary element taking advantage of the opportunity, using a false name, attempting to disrupt the party system, and engaging in disruptive conspiracies. As this concerns party discipline, in addition to reporting it to the higher authorities for thorough investigation, we hereby solemnly declare our denial of the illegal meeting and its so-called Party Affairs Improvement Committee, to rectify the public perception and avoid confusion. We hope for public discernment. The First, Second, Fifth, Sixth, Ninth, and Tenth District Executive Committees of Shanghai Special Municipality."

Meeting of the Executive Committee of the Municipal Party Affairs Improvement Committee

The Executive Committee of the Shanghai Special Municipality Party Affairs Improvement Committee of the Kuomintang of China held its first Executive Committee meeting at 8:00 PM yesterday. All committee members were present, with Wang Hanliang as chairman and Xing Wan as secretary. After the chairman's report, the meeting immediately began to discuss important resolutions as follows: (1) Regarding the proposal of the General Assembly to support Mr. Wang Jingwei's National Salvation Conference and advocate the publication of a declaration, it was resolved to approve it. (2) Regarding the General Assembly's resolution to oppose secret diplomacy and severely punish Zhang Xueliang, and how to implement it, it was resolved to issue a circular telegram. (3) Regarding the General Assembly's resolution to send representatives to express sympathy to the students of Peking University and National Central University who were beaten, it was resolved to appoint comrades Zhu Chengzi and Zhang Juansheng to go. (4) Regarding the General Assembly's resolution on how to implement the punishment of the principal and accomplices who suppressed the people's movement, it was resolved to first appoint personnel to investigate. (5) Regarding the drafting of the provisional regulations of the organization, it was resolved to appoint comrades Chen Baixin and Li Zheng to be responsible for drafting and submitting it to the next meeting for revision. (6) Regarding the drafting of the people's movement plan, it was resolved to appoint comrades Zhang Tinghao and Qian Zanting to draft and submit it to the next meeting for revision. (7) Regarding the proposal to publish a declaration by the committee, it was resolved to approve it. The meeting adjourned.

Joint Declaration of All Labor Unions in the City Regarding the Current Situation

The Municipal Party Headquarters Must Be Reorganized

Oppose Reorganization, Support the Party Affairs Improvement Committee

More than seventy labor unions in this city, including the Municipal Postal Workers Union, Postal Service Union, Fourth District Cigarette Union, Sixth District Water and Electricity Union, Seventh District Cotton Textile Union, Dyeing Industry Union, Pharmaceutical Industry Union, Steamboat Carpentry Union, Pharmaceutical Trade Union, Newspaper Delivery Union, First District Sanitation Union, Fifth District Match Union, Fourth District Transportation Union, Qin Industry Union, Silk Finishing Office of the Dyeing Industry Union, Leather Manufacturing Union, First District Shipbuilding Union, Second District Cotton Textile Union, Hat Making Union, Civil Steamboat Carpentry Union, Wine Making Union, Fifth District Shipbuilding Union, Ninth District Soap and Pharmaceutical Union, Egg Industry Union, Sixth District Cotton Textile Union, Sixth District Knitting Industry Union, Fourth District Sanitation Union, Ink Making Union, Garment Making Union, Dongjiadu Ferry Union, Fifth District Cotton Spinning Union, Fragrance Industry Union, Sanpin Dyeing Industry Union, First District Shipbuilding Union, Second District Silk Weaving Union, First District Rubber Industry Union, Silk Spitting Industry Union, Second District Knitting Industry Union, Fourth District Silk Weaving Union, Sixth District Public Bus Industry Union, Sauce Industry Union, etc., yesterday convened an emergency joint meeting regarding the incident at the Student Federation and the recent party affairs disputes, and issued a solemn declaration. As in the recent December 9th incident at the Shanghai Student Federation, the responsible persons of the municipal party headquarters and the municipal Public Security Bureau brazenly and madly used brutal methods unseen in the world, binding and beating students, forming an unprecedented tragedy, and creating a stain on the history of the revolution. The foundation of the party has been shaken, and the prestige of the party has been swept away. The root cause of past failures is not in the Three People's Principles themselves, but in the vast majority of shameless people who use the party for personal gain, commit evil deeds recklessly, and allow the country to be destroyed and the principles to be abandoned, while personal interests must be fought for. The party and the principles have been gradually eroded and corrupted by these evil forces for years. Those people conspire for personal gain and engage in malfeasance, ultimately blaming the party. They hold the power but blame the party for the consequences. The pioneers of our party have painfully pointed this out. Today, the eastern provinces have been brutally trampled, the Japanese invaders are advancing step by step, and the poor people are suffering and crying out, all wanting to serve the country and die, but are being taken advantage of by shameless and unconscionable people, who seize the opportunity to satisfy their selfish desires for short-term committee positions, while ignoring the party's laws and the country's survival. Alas, the late Premier Sun Yat-sen initiated the Three People's Principles to save the country through the party, but less than seven years after his death, the country has been injured and the party has been robbed. If he has a spirit in the afterlife, can he not weep and shed tears? This association laments the imminent destruction of the country and the decay of the party's governance. It will abide by the government's intentions and be a vanguard for all sectors of society. Now that the situation has reached this point, it is no longer time for us to sit idly by. Therefore, we sincerely appeal to our beloved compatriots throughout the country, 'To resist foreign aggression, we must first secure the country internally.' This is a precedent in history. The way to secure the country internally is to save the country, and the way to save the party is to eliminate traitors. The past municipal party headquarters must be reorganized. However, taking advantage of the resignation of all members of the municipal party headquarters, the so-called Party Affairs Improvement Committee has been organized. In terms of procedure, it does not conform to the principles of democratic centralism. In terms of personnel selection, most are either former members of the municipal party headquarters or people of lost moral character. This kind of improper combination can only shake the faith of the party and is not enough to lead the people of the city. For the sake of saving the party, this association vows to deny this meeting and hopes that all revolutionary people in the city will unanimously advocate and rise up to correct it. This is the first point. Young students, with ardent blood and sincerity, do not complain about hunger or cold, and call for the nation. Their patriotic spirit and determination have created a new record in the history of the student movement. However, the authorities insult them with dirty hearts, which is heartbreaking. We hope that the officials who are ordered to be responsible for investigating this case will conduct a thorough investigation impartially to calm public anger. This is the second point. Since the September 18th Incident, months have passed, and the authorities have been negligent before and after the event. If this continues, the situation will become even more difficult to manage. This association still maintains its previous proposal and urges Commander-in-Chief Chiang Kai-shek to swear an oath and go north immediately to recover the lost territories by force, and to urge the Guangdong committee members to go to the capital as soon as possible to actively prepare for self-defense, reorganize national affairs, and revitalize party affairs. This is the third point. These three points are essential for saving the party and the country, and cannot be delayed. If the government authorities continue to delay, act like barbarians, and remain unrepentant, ignoring the calls of the people and failing to save the country from danger, then the people of the whole country will surely rise up together. The time is critical, and it is fleeting. This association leads all workers in the city and works together with our beloved compatriots from all walks of life to achieve our goals. We hereby declare."

Gentry and Merchants Host the Student Community Yesterday

Willing for Students' Fathers and Elder Brothers to Assume Responsibility for Saving the Nation

Yesterday at 3:00 PM, gentry and merchants Yu Qiaqing, Shi Liangcai, Wang Xiaolai, Qin Runqing, Yuan Ludeng, Li Cishan, Xu Jiqing, Zhang Gongquan, Zhang Xiaolin, Du Yuesheng, Liu Hongsheng, Lu Bohong, Xu Xinliu, Wei Tingrong, Hu Mengjia, Chen Guangfu, and Lin Kanghou, gathered the principals of various universities and middle schools in Shanghai and the Shanghai Student Anti-Japanese National Salvation United Association, the Student Anti-Japanese National Salvation United Association of various middle schools, and two student representatives from various middle schools in the city at the Shaoxing Fellow Countrymen Association on Avenue Edward VII to hold a discussion meeting. Those who attended included Liu Zhan'en of Shanghai University, He Shizhen of Chih Tze College, Chu Minyi of the Sino-French National Institute of Technology, Xu Peihuang of the Central University Business School, Hu Shuhua of Tongji University, Wang Jingqi of Labor University, Chu Huiseng of Law School, College of Law and Politics, China Women's Physical Education School, Southeast Medical College, National Conservatory of Music, Shanghai Art College, Liangjiang Women's Physical Education School, Daxia University, Guanghua University, China Vocational School, Surveying and Mapping School, Gongshi School, Cai Guo Jingluan, Quanzhang Middle School, Chen Guichen, Minzhi School, Chu Shichao of Shanghai Girls' Middle School, Shenmei Girls' Middle School, Hubbei Middle School, Choufan Girls' Middle School, Sanyu Middle School, Yucai Middle School, Yuqing Middle School, Xinmin Middle School, Guangdong Middle School, Shibei Middle School, Huideng Girls' Middle School, Nanyang Girls' Middle School, Mingde Middle School, Dongwu Second Middle School, Chengzong Middle School, Xiejin Middle School, Nanfang Middle School, Qinghua Middle School, Huiling Middle School, Nanyang Normal Middle School, McLaren Middle School, Fudan Benchen Middle School, Guangzhao Middle School, Qingxin Middle School, Jianguo Middle School, Junyi Middle School, Daxia Middle School, Datong Affiliated Middle School, Huaisi Junior High School, Zhirenyong Middle School, Peiming Girls' Middle School, Minsheng Middle School, Shanghai Provincial Middle School, Minli Girls' Middle School, Minguo Girls' Middle School, Qixiu Girls' Middle School, Lida College, and principals and students from about 200 schools such as Zhaoji, Huahua, YMCA, Dongfang, Zhengxin, Zhengfeng, Qianye, Tiehua, Aiqun, Pudong, etc. Yu Qiaqing first gave an opening speech, Wang Xiaolai said that all sectors should fulfill their responsibilities in the anti-Japanese incident. Lin Kanghou said that the garrison headquarters and the Public Security Bureau in Shanghai are still lacking responsible persons, and the financial sector is showing instability. Shi Liangcai said that the fundamental solution to resist Japan is to seek China's prosperity. Agricultural science, industrial mechanization, and large-scale companies should be established in the industry to enrich the people and make China strong. Li Cishan said that China is vast and difficult to unify. Countries in the world, such as the United States and Russia, are federal states. In the past, Yuan Shikai and Wu Peifu wanted to unify by force, but could not. Therefore, considering the situation, a federal system is also appropriate. Chu Fucheng said that the students' strike is due to the lack of a study environment. However, if the children are to study with peace of mind, their fathers and elder brothers must assume responsibility for saving the nation. Hu Shuhua also advocated that the schools resume classes first. Lin Kanghou also said that it is admirable that the students are engaged in the national salvation movement. However, in the current unstable situation, one should not neglect to prevent the Communist Party and Japanese spies from taking the opportunity to disturb the situation, and should be cautious. We deeply hope that a unified and responsible government will be realized immediately. It would be fortunate if we did not have to wave flags and shout again, and we would like to meet with you again soon to see the success of this hope. Then, a representative of Fudan students explained the petition process. Representatives of the Anti-Japanese Association of various middle schools stated that their fathers and elder brothers would be deeply comforted if they could assume responsibility for saving the nation, but they were deeply concerned that they might not be able to fulfill their responsibilities. The meeting adjourned at 6:00 PM.

Zou Lu Delivers a Speech Responding to the National Salvation Conference

Jointly Plan to Deal with the Current National Crisis

Elect Representatives to Participate in Politics

End the Tutelage and Realize Constitutional Government

Since Mr. Wang Jingwei launched the National Salvation Conference, responses have sprung up from all sides. Yesterday, Guangdong representative Zou Haibin also delivered a speech regarding this matter, saying, "Since Mr. Wang Jingwei launched the National Salvation Conference, there has been unanimous support from all sides. Mr. Hu Zhantang has supplemented the organizational composition and other aspects, and his eagerness to promote its success is especially evident. I also absolutely support Mr. Wang Jingwei's proposal. However, in this critical period, I intend to expand its nature and responsibilities. The so-called expansion of the nature means that this conference should not only deal with the current situation, but also determine the future political system, combining the nature of both the National Conference and the National Assembly as defined by the Premier. Therefore, its responsibilities should focus on the following three points: (1) Jointly plan to deal with the current national crisis. (2) Elect representatives to participate in central politics. (3) Serve as the pivot for ending the tutelage and realizing constitutional government. There is a need to explain the nature of this conference. Internal and external troubles have reached their peak today. The reasons for this are varied, but political autocracy and separation from the public, where the public does not know the measures taken by the government and increasingly distrust it, are major reasons. Therefore, the current national crisis requires the joint efforts of the people, and future politics should be shouldered by the people. Especially in this critical time of survival, constitutional government must be implemented as soon as possible. If held separately, it would be prolonged and unable to respond to this national crisis. Since the representatives are elected by the people, there seems to be no need for such a redundant move. Therefore, the nature and proposals of this National Salvation Conference embody the meaning of both the Premier's National Conference and National Assembly. The three responsibilities of this conference can be explained separately. (1) Dealing with the current national crisis has been elaborated by Mr. Wang Jingwei. Indeed, in recent years, domestic and foreign affairs have not satisfied the people and have not been understood by the people. In terms of diplomacy, why has the withdrawal of Japanese troops from Jinan been delayed? Why did the Sino-Soviet war occur? Why have there been hundreds of cases involving the Northeast? Since the Japanese invasion, why has there been no resistance? Why has the establishment of a neutral zone in Jinzhou and the request for joint administration of Tianjin been widely reported in Chinese and foreign newspapers? In terms of domestic affairs, how have the Communists caused such a phenomenon? Why has the suppression of the Communists become more intense? Why has the national debt exceeded 100 million? Where is the purpose of all the money? Floods are indeed natural disasters, but why has the prevention and disaster relief work in various provinces suddenly been abandoned? As for all construction, it is nothing more than empty words, and the livelihood of the people has reached its limit. All of this makes the people feel lost. The people do not understand, and the autocracy is getting worse, further isolating the people. This is why the recent national crisis has led the people to passionately resist foreign aggression, while students and workers have mostly criticized the government. If there is no agency to allow the people to participate in and understand all politics, it will be impossible for them to have confidence and work together to overcome the national crisis. (2) Electing representatives to participate in political affairs. Because of political autocracy, the people are alienated and do not trust the government. If the revolution is separated from the people, it will surely fail. To ensure that the government and the people are not alienated, it is essential to have the people elect representatives to participate in central political affairs. This is why the Founding Program stipulates that during the period of tutelage, 'after the establishment of a local autonomous government in each county, one representative may be elected to form a representative assembly to participate in central political affairs.' The current peace conference also pays attention to the participation of national representatives in political affairs, which Mr. Sun Zhegeng has clearly stated. When the people suspect the government of political issues, there is no other way to make the people understand the government and trust the government. At the same time, the government cannot combine with the people and stand together on the revolutionary front. (3) Ending the tutelage and realizing constitutional government. Although it has been called tutelage for years, nothing has been done in accordance with the Premier's methods for the period of tutelage. Instead, the name of tutelage has been used to create responsibility for autocracy. This is why the people have been criticizing the tutelage recently. Moreover, the matter of tutelage is most prone to despotism. Unless it is carried out with the Premier's selfless spirit, it will inevitably lead to abuses. As the saying goes, 'If you have the ambition of Yi Yin, you can do it; if you do not have the ambition of Yi Yin, you should not do it.' Mr. Sun Zhegeng advocates realizing constitutional government as soon as possible. I believe that his political proposals over the years have been along the same lines. If constitutional government can be realized as soon as possible, and the people of the whole country can concentrate their will and talents under constitutional government to save the current national crisis and determine the future political system, this will be the Premier's will to complete the revolution and the eternal achievement of the Republic of China. The above are my supplementary opinions on Mr. Wang Jingwei's National Salvation Conference. Mr. Wang Jingwei is currently drafting an organizational plan for the National Salvation Conference, providing detailed rules and regulations. There will surely be more detailed and better methods to meet the expectations of the nation and lay the foundation for the Republic of China. We are willing to wait and see with the people."

Responses to Wang Jingwei's Telegram

Jiangsu Promotion Association Telegram: The Jiangsu Promotion Association for the National Salvation Conference sent a telegram, saying, "To all people's organizations and newspapers: Since the Japanese invasion of the eastern provinces, the situation has become increasingly urgent for several months. However, the government has not made active preparations and has not informed the people of the coping strategies. All our compatriots are saddened. We believe that at this critical moment, it is not enough to talk about saving the nation without concentrating the power of the people throughout the country. Recently, we read Mr. Wang Jingwei's telegram, advocating the organization of a National Salvation Conference, with each people's organization sending representatives to jointly plan to deal with the national crisis, which is the only good way to save the country. We have established the Jiangsu Promotion Association for the National Salvation Conference today, vowing to support Mr. Wang's proposal with all our strength and urge its early realization. We hereby send this telegram for your attention. Respectfully, the Jiangsu Promotion Association for the National Salvation Conference."

Anhui Youth National Salvation Corps Telegram: The Anhui Youth National Salvation Corps in Shanghai sent a telegram, saying, "Foreign troubles are pressing, unification has not been achieved, the country is about to perish, and the people have no place to die. Mr. Wang Jingwei believes that the realization of democratic politics is essential to save the party and the country from danger, and therefore initiated the National Salvation Conference. His words are incisive and fit the feelings of the people. There is no other way to revive China. We hope that all compatriots throughout the country will rise up together. In addition to sending a separate telegram to Mr. Wang to announce the organizational plan and detailed regulations, we send this telegram first, and earnestly pray."
